  differently wrt. code generation.%

\isacommand{class}\isamarkupfalse%
\ semiring{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}operations\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ semiring{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bits\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeyword{fixes}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}and{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}AND{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{6}}{\isadigit{4}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ or\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}OR{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{5}}{\isadigit{9}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ xor\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}XOR{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{5}}{\isadigit{9}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ mask\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ set{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ unset{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ flip{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ drop{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}nat\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeyword{assumes}\ bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}and{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iff\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}simps{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ AND\ b{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymand}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}or{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iff\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}simps{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ OR\ b{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymor}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}xor{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iff\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}simps{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ XOR\ b{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymnoteq}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ mask{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}exp{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}minus{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}{\isadigit{1}}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}mask\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharcircum}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ set{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}or{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}set{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ OR\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ {\isadigit{1}}{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}unset{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}iff\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}simps{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}unset{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ m\ a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isasymlongleftrightarrow}\ bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymand}\ m\ {\isasymnoteq}\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ flip{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}xor{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}flip{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ XOR\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ {\isadigit{1}}{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}mult{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharcircum}{\kern0pt}\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ drop{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}div{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}drop{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ div\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharcircum}{\kern0pt}\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}eq{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}mod{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacartoucheopen}take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ mod\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharcircum}{\kern0pt}\ n{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
\isakeyword{begin}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
We want the bitwise operations to bind slightly weaker
  than \isa{{\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}} and \isa{{\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}}.

  Logically, \isa{push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit},
  \isa{drop{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit} and \isa{take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit} are just aliases; having them
  as separate operations makes proofs easier, otherwise proof automation
  would fiddle with concrete expressions \isa{{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup } in a way obfuscating the basic
  algebraic relationships between those operations.

  For the sake of code generation operations 
  are specified as definitional class operations,
  taking into account that specific instances of these can be implemented
  differently wrt. code generation.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{sublocale}\isamarkupfalse%
\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}and{\isachardoublequoteclose}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ semilattice\ {\isacartoucheopen}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}AND{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacartoucheclose}\isanewline
%

\ \ %
\endisadelimproof

\endisatagproof

\isacommand{lemmas}\isamarkupfalse%

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
For the sake of code generation \isa{NOT} is specified as
  definitional class operation.  Note that \isa{NOT} has no
  sensible definition for unlimited but only positive bit strings
  (type \isa{nat}).%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsubsection{Key ideas of bit operations%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
When formalizing bit operations, it is tempting to represent
bit values as explicit lists over a binary type. This however
is a bad idea, mainly due to the inherent ambiguities in
representation concerning repeating leading bits.

Hence this approach avoids such explicit lists altogether
following an algebraic path:

%
\begin{itemize}%
\item Bit values are represented by numeric types: idealized
unbounded bit values can be represented by type \isa{int},
bounded bit values by quotient types over \isa{int}.

\item (A special case are idealized unbounded bit values ending
in \isa{{\isadigit{0}}} which can be represented by type \isa{nat} but
only support a restricted set of operations).

\item From this idea follows that

%
\begin{itemize}%
\item multiplication by \isa{{\isadigit{2}}} is a bit shift to the left and

\item division by \isa{{\isadigit{2}}} is a bit shift to the right.%
\end{itemize}

\item Concerning bounded bit values, iterated shifts to the left
may result in eliminating all bits by shifting them all
beyond the boundary.  The property \isa{{\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup \ {\isasymnoteq}\ {\isadigit{0}}}
represents that \isa{n} is \emph{not} beyond that boundary.

\item The projection on a single bit is then \isa{bit\ a\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ odd\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ div\ {\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup {\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}.

\item This leads to the most fundamental properties of bit values:

%
\begin{itemize}%
\item Equality rule: \isa{{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymAnd}n{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ possible{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ TYPE{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}int{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ bit\ a\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ b}

\item Induction rule: \isa{{\isasymlbrakk}{\isasymAnd}a{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ a\ div\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ P\ a{\isacharsemicolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymAnd}a\ b{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymlbrakk}P\ a{\isacharsemicolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}of{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bool\ b\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ div\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a{\isasymrbrakk}\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ P\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}of{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bool\ b\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isasymrbrakk}\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ P\ a}%
\end{itemize}

\item Typical operations are characterized as follows:

%
\begin{itemize}%
\item Singleton \isa{n}th bit: \isa{{\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup }

\item Bit mask upto bit \isa{n}: \isa{mask\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup \ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}}

\item Left shift: \isa{push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup }

\item Right shift: \isa{drop{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ div\ {\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup }

\item Truncation: \isa{take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ mod\ {\isadigit{2}}\isactrlbsup n\isactrlesup }

\item Negation: \isa{bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}NOT\ a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymnot}\ {\isasymnot}\ possible{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ TYPE{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}int{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isasymand}\ {\isasymnot}\ bit\ a\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}

\item And: \isa{bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ AND\ b{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymand}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}

\item Or: \isa{bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ OR\ b{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymor}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}

\item Xor: \isa{bit\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a\ XOR\ b{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ n\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}bit\ a\ n\ {\isasymnoteq}\ bit\ b\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}

\item Set a single bit: \isa{set{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ OR\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ {\isadigit{1}}}

\item Unset a single bit: \isa{unset{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ AND\ NOT\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ {\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}

\item Flip a single bit: \isa{flip{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ a\ XOR\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ {\isadigit{1}}}

\item Signed truncation, or modulus centered around \isa{{\isadigit{0}}}: \isa{signed{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a\ OR\ of{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bool\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}bit\ a\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ NOT\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}mask\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}}

\item Bit concatenation: \isa{concat{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ k\ l\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ k\ OR\ push{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ l}

\item (Bounded) conversion from and to a list of bits: \isa{horner{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}sum\ of{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bool\ {\isadigit{2}}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}map\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}bit\ a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}{\isadigit{0}}{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}{\isacharless}{\kern0pt}n{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ take{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}bit\ n\ a}%
\end{itemize}%
\end{itemize}%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{no{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}notation}\isamarkupfalse%
\isanewline
\ \ not\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacartoucheopen}NOT{\isacartoucheclose}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}and{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}AND{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{6}}{\isadigit{4}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ or\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}OR{\isacartoucheclose}\ \ {\isadigit{5}}{\isadigit{9}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ xor\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}XOR{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{5}}{\isadigit{9}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\isanewline
\isacommand{bundle}\isamarkupfalse%
\ bit{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}operations{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}syntax\isanewline
\isakeyword{begin}\isanewline
\isanewline
\isacommand{notation}\isamarkupfalse%
\isanewline
\ \ not\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacartoucheopen}NOT{\isacartoucheclose}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}and{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}AND{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{6}}{\isadigit{4}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ or\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}OR{\isacartoucheclose}\ \ {\isadigit{5}}{\isadigit{9}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ xor\ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeyword{infixr}\ {\isacartoucheopen}XOR{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{5}}{\isadigit{9}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\isanewline
\isacommand{end}\isamarkupfalse%
